CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_absemce` (
  `ABSENCE_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Absence Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `ABSENCE_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the absence code',
  `ABSENCE_DESCRIPTION` varchar(500) NULL COMMENT 'Detailed description about the absece code',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`ABSENCE_CODE`),
  UNIQUE KEY `ABSENCE_NAME` (`ABSENCE_NAME`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_challenge_group` (

  `CG_max_CREDITABLE` varchar(10) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Group ',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`CG_CODE`),
  UNIQUE KEY `CG_NAME` (`CG_NAME`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `employee` (
  `ROW_ID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `EMP_FIRST_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee First Name',
  `EMP_LAST_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee Last Name',
  `EMP_PAN_NO` varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee PAN No',
  `EMP_GPF_NO` varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee GPF No',
  `EMP_CPS_NO` varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee CPS No',
  `EMP_GENDER` varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee Gernder',
  `EMP_BIRTH_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee Date of Birth',
  `EMP_PERSONAL_NO` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Employee Personal No',
  `EMP_BEGIN_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee Start Date of Employment',
  `EMP_END_DT` date NOT NULL DEFAULT '9999-12-31' COMMENT 'Employee End Date of Employment',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`ROW_ID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `EMP_PAN_NO` (`EMP_PAN_NO`),
  UNIQUE KEY `EMP_GPF_NO` (`EMP_GPF_NO`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `ROW_ID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `EMPLOYEE_ROW_ID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT 'FK of the Employee Table',
  `DECIPLINE_CASE_NO` varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Case Number of Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_CODE` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Disciplinary action code for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_SOURCE_CODE` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Source of Deciplinary Action for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_OFFENCE_DT` date NULL COMMENT 'Date of Deciplinary Action taken  for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_STATUS_CODE` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Status of Deciplinary Action for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_OUTCOME_CODE` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Outcome of Deciplinary Action for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_FROM_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Action from Date for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_ACTION_TO_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Action to Date for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_SENTENCE_PENALTY` float (10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' NOT NULL COMMENT 'Disciplinary action pelanty for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_SENTENCE_PERIOD` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Disciplinary action Period for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_SENTENCE_PERIOD_UNIT` varchar(20) NULL COMMENT 'Disciplinary action Unit for Employee',
  `DECIPLINE_BEGIN_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee Start Date for personal info',
  `DECIPLINE_END_DT` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee End Date for personal info',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  PRIMARY KEY (`ROW_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_personal_subarea` (
  `PSA_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `PSA_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the sub area',
  `PSA_CAPITAL` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Capital of subarea about the Challenge Type',
  `PSA_GENERATION` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Capital of subarea about the Challenge Type',
  `PSA_TRANSMISSION` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Capital of subarea about the Challenge Type',
  `PSA_WINTER` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Capital of subarea about the Challenge Type',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
  ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_personal_area_subarea` (
  `PA_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `PSA_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
  ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_group` (
  `EG_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `EG_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EG_DESCRIPTION` varchar(500) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Detailed description about the Challenge Type',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
 ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Employee Group and subgroup EG_CODE to EGS_CODE mapping
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_group_subgroup` (
  `EG_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee group code Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `EGS_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Employee sub group  Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `EGS_CLASS` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Employee class Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `EGS_CGROUP` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `EGS_HR_COUNTRY_GROUP` varchar(50)  NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `EGS_ALLOWED` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
  ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_actions` (
  `EA_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Action Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `EA_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_FC` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_CUS_REF` varchar(50) NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_EMLOYMENT` varchar(50)  NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_SPEC_PAYMENT` varchar(50)  NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_CHECK` varchar(50)  NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_P` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',
  `EA_PA` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'User Friendly Name Given to the Challenge Type',

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_actions_reasons` (
  `EA_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',  
  `EAR_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Contract Type Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_education_branch` (
  `BRANCH_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Branch Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `BRANCH_DESCRIPTION` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Branch code description with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `m_employee_education_code_branch` (
  `QUALIFICATION_LEVEL` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Qualification Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `BRANCH_CODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Branch Code with not spl chars and underscore only hyphens allowed',
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'Record Status set values for BLOCKED, ACTIVE, INACTIVE, SUSPENDED DELETED etc, use -ve values for negetive status.',
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  `CREATED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MODIFIED_BY` varchar(50) NULL,
  `MODIFIED_DATE` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
